news_event = { #1 - Inauguration of Tjarda van Starkenborgh
	id = holhisind_news.1
	title = holhisind_news.1.t
	desc = holhisind_news.1.d
	picture = GFX_event_ins_pen_and_paper
	
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = holhisind_news.1.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = INS
				tag = HOL
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holhisind_news.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = INS
					tag = HOL
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_ideology = moderatism
				has_country_leader_ideology = centrism
				has_country_leader_ideology = despotism
				has_country_leader_ideology = conservatism
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = holhisind_news.1.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = INS
					tag = HOL
					has_country_leader_ideology = moderatism
					has_country_leader_ideology = centrism
					has_country_leader_ideology = despotism
					has_country_leader_ideology = conservatism
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = { #3 - Fall of Batavia
	id = holhisind_news.3
	title = holhisind_news.3.t
	desc = holhisind_news.3.d
	picture = GFX_event_ins_japan_batavia
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {
		335 = { is_owned_by = INS }
		335 = { is_controlled_by = JAP }
		JAP = {
			has_war_with = INS
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = fall_of_batavia_ins }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = fall_of_batavia_ins
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = holhisind_news.3.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				TAG = INS
				is_in_faction_with = INS
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holhisind_news.3.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				TAG = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = holhisind_news.3.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TAG = INS
				TAG = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = INS
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #1 - De Jonge 61st birthday
	id = holhis_indonesia.1
	title = holhis_indonesia.1.t
	desc = holhis_indonesia.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_de_jonge_aging

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		has_government = neutrality
		date > 1936.01.02
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		NOT = { has_country_flag = INS_de_jonge_resigned }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = holhis_indonesia.1.a
		set_country_flag = INS_needs_governor
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = holhis_indonesia_locks_discourage_tt
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holhis_indonesia.1.b
		HOL = {
			HOL_johannes_theodorus_furstner = {
				set_nationality = INS
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = INS_needs_governor
		set_country_flag = INS_furstner_stay_flag
		custom_effect_tooltip = holhis_indonesia_open_discourage_tt
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #2 - "There so much good to be done more" book release 
	id = holhis_indonesia.2
	title = holhis_indonesia.2.t
	desc = holhis_indonesia.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_helsdingen_book

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		date > 1936.02.20
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = { #good book
		name = holhis_indonesia.2.a
		add_political_power = 5
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}

	option = { #endorse it
		name = holhis_indonesia.2.b
		add_political_power = 10
		add_war_support = 0.02
		add_stability = -0.01
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = { #3 - Van Mook and co attends the expo
	id = holhis_indonesia.3
	title = holhis_indonesia.3.t
	desc = holhis_indonesia.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_van_mook_flight

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		has_government = neutrality
		date > 1936.02.03
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		USA = {
			exists = yes
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = INS
			}
		}
	}

    option = { #safe trip
		name = holhis_indonesia.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = holhis_indonesia.4 days = 150 }
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = holhis_indonesia.5 days = 150 }
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = holhis_indonesia.6 days = 150 }
				}
			}
		}
    }
}

		}

		}
    }

country_event = { #8 - Raad van State choose de Jonge's successor
	id = holhis_indonesia.8
	title = holhis_indonesia.8.t

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.8.d_1
		trigger = {
			INS = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = INS_furstner_stay_flag }
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.8.d_2
		trigger = {
			INS = {
				has_country_flag = INS_furstner_stay_flag
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_de_jonge_aging

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = holhis_indonesia.8.a #A.W.L. Tjarda
		set_country_flag = HOL_choose_tjarda_flag
		INS = { country_event = { id = holhis_indonesia.9 days = 56 } }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				INS = {
					focus_progress = {
						focus = INS_discourage_democratic_reforms
						progress > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holhis_indonesia.8.b #Furstner
		set_country_flag = HOL_choose_furstner_flag
		INS = { country_event = { id = holhis_indonesia.9 days = 56 } }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				INS = {
					focus_progress = {
						focus = INS_discourage_democratic_reforms
						progress > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #9 - Dutch Raad choose Tjarda
	id = holhis_indonesia.9
	title = holhis_indonesia.9.t
	desc = holhis_indonesia.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_tjarda_jonge_handover

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Hurrah
		name = holhis_indonesia.9.a
		set_country_flag = INS_de_jonge_resigned
		promote_character = INS_a_t_van_starkenborgh_stachouwer
		retire_character = INS_bonifacius_de_jonge
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = INS_neutrality_party_volksraad_long
			name = INS_neutrality_party_volksraad
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = INS_democratic_party_volksraad_long
			name = INS_democratic_party_volksraad
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { 
				if = {
					limit = {
						exists = yes
						has_capitulated = no
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = HOL
							is_neighbor_of = INS
							tag = JAP
							is_subject_of = HOL
							is_subject_of = ENG
							is_subject_of = FRA
							is_subject_of = BEL
							is_southwest_pacific_state = yes
							num_subjects > 0
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						hours = 12
						id = holhisind_news.1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #90 - Dutch Raad choose Furstner
	id = holhis_indonesia.90
	title = holhis_indonesia.90.t
	desc = holhis_indonesia.90.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Hurrah
		name = holhis_indonesia.90.a
		set_country_flag = INS_de_jonge_resigned
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = HOL_johannes_theodorus_furstner
			country_leader = {
				desc = HOL_johannes_furstner_govgen_desc
				expire = "1970.9.15"
				ideology = despotism
				traits = {
					strongman_indies
				}
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		retire_character = INS_bonifacius_de_jonge
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = INS_neutrality_party_volksraad_long
			name = INS_neutrality_party_volksraad
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = INS_democratic_party_volksraad_long
			name = INS_democratic_party_volksraad
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { 
				if = {
					limit = {
						exists = yes
						has_capitulated = no
						OR = {
							is_neighbor_of = HOL
							is_neighbor_of = INS
							tag = JAP
							is_subject_of = HOL
							is_subject_of = ENG
							is_subject_of = FRA
							is_subject_of = BEL
							is_southwest_pacific_state = yes
							num_subjects > 0
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						hours = 12
						id = holhisind_news.11
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #11 - Hamengkubuwono Eighth's passing
	id = holhis_indonesia.11
	title = holhis_indonesia.11.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_hamengkoeboewono_ninth_coronation

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.11.d_1
		trigger = {
			has_idea = INS_hubertus_van_mook
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.11.d_2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_idea = INS_hubertus_van_mook }
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Soekarno"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.11.d_3
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Soekarno"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		date > 1939.10.22
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_government = fascism
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 100 }

	option = {
		name = holhis_indonesia.11.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_hamengkoeboewono_eighth
			}
			set_country_flag = INS_hamengkoeboewono_invited_flag
			remove_ideas = INS_hamengkoeboewono_eighth
			add_ideas = INS_hamengkoeboewono_ninth
		}
		retire_character = INS_hamengkoeboewono_eighth
		set_country_flag = INS_hamengkoeboewono_viii_passed
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = INS_reestablish_royal_houses
			}
			add_corps_commander_role = {
				character = INS_hamengkoeboewono_ninth
				traits = { politically_connected }
				skill = 1
				attack_skill = 1
				defense_skill = 1
				planning_skill = 1
				logistics_skill = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			1018 = {
				add_manpower = -1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #12 - INS new capital
	id = holhis_indonesia.12
	title = holhis_indonesia.12.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_batavia_parade

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.12.d_1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = INS_continue_reform
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = INS_discourage_democratic_reforms
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = INS_revive_spirit_1926 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.12.d_2
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = INS_revive_spirit_1926
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = INS_soekarno
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.12.d_3
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = INS_soekarno
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #keep Batavia
		name = holhis_indonesia.12.a
		set_country_flag = INS_renew_batavia
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = INS_build_capital_1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				industrial_complex < 12

country_event = { #16 - Hart Retires
	id = holhis_indonesia.16
	title = holhis_indonesia.16.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_hart

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.16.d_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = INS_reinstate_stuwgroep
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.16.d_2
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = INS_reinstate_stuwgroep
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		has_character = INS_george_hart
		OR = {
			date > 1943.08.08
			check_variable = { var = INS_JAP_trade value = 2 compare = greater_than }
			has_completed_focus = INS_emerald_equator
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = { #Accepted (van Mook)
		name = holhis_indonesia.16.a

		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = INS_reinstate_stuwgroep }
		}

		set_country_flag = INS_hart_retired
		set_country_flag = INS_van_mook_coi
		hidden_effect = {
			INS_hubertus_van_mook = {
				add_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = coi_mook
				}
				remove_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = skilled_negotiator
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_george_hart
			}
			deactivate_advisor = INS_george_hart
			activate_advisor = INS_hubertus_van_mook
		}
		retire_character = INS_george_hart
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	option = { #Accepted (Hoogstraten)
		name = holhis_indonesia.16.b

		trigger = {
			 has_completed_focus = INS_reinstate_stuwgroep
		}

		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 25

		set_country_flag = INS_hart_retired
		set_country_flag = INS_hoogstraten_coi

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_george_hart
			}
			deactivate_advisor = INS_george_hart
			activate_advisor = INS_hoogstraten
		}
		retire_character = INS_george_hart

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

	option = { #pls work more for a bit
		name = holhis_indonesia.16.c

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = INS_hart_overworked_flag
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		INS_george_hart = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_country_leader_traits = {
					remove = captain_of_industry
					add = coi_hart
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = coi_hart
				}
				remove_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = captain_of_industry
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_hart_overworked_flag
			country_event = { id = holhis_indonesia.16 days = 630 random_days = 100 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #17 - Chindo Riots
	id = holhis_indonesia.17
	title = holhis_indonesia.17.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_sinpo

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.17.d_1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_1
				has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_2
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = holhis_indonesia.17.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_1
					has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_2
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		OR = {
			has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_1
			has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_2
			has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_3
		}
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				focus_progress = {
					focus = INS_strict_neutrality_china_war
					progress > 0
				}
				focus_progress = {
					focus = INS_support_china_war
					progress > 0
				}
				has_country_flag = INS_ally_china_war_flag
				has_country_flag = INS_neutral_china_war_flag
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			is_literally_china = yes
			any_enemy_country = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
			has_capitulated = no
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 175 }

	option = { #Support
		name = holhis_indonesia.17.a
		add_stability = -0.075
		add_war_support = -0.075
		set_country_flag = INS_ally_china_war_flag
		JAP = {
			clr_country_flag = JAP_declare_war_indies_banned
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_literally_china = yes
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = medium_increase
			}
		}
		HOL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = small_decrease
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = large_decrease
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_1
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_japanese_investment_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_2
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_japanese_investment_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_japanese_investment_3
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_japanese_investment_3
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Crack them
		name = holhis_indonesia.17.b
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_country_flag = INS_neutral_china_war_flag
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_literally_china = yes
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = small_decrease
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = CHI
				OR = {
					original_tag = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = medium_increase
			}
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = INS_mission_japanese_aid
			days = 105
		}
		remove_ideas = INS_nv_merbaboe
		set_country_flag = INS_merbaboe_quits_flag

country_event = { #54 - The Queen returns home
	id = holhis_indonesia.54
	title = holhis_indonesia.54.t
	desc = holhis_indonesia.54.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_hol_wilhelmina_speech

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = {
			flag = INS_wilhelmina_tropical_holiday_flag
			days > 180
		}
		NOT = {
			HOL = {
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = holhis_indonesia.54.a #Long Live the Queen!!!
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = INS_indies_dominion_act
			days = 3650
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = hol_puppet_neutrality_var
				value = party_popularity@neutrality
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
					is_subject_of = HOL
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
				}
				HOL = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = INS
						autonomous_state = autonomy_colony
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 100
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = hol_puppet_neutrality_var
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
					is_subject_of = HOL
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				}
				HOL = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = INS
						autonomous_state = autonomy_colony
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 100
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = hol_puppet_neutrality_var
				}
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = INS_wilhelmina_tropical_holiday_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			INS = {
				HOL_wilhelmina = {
					set_nationality = HOL
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Navair 4 - Asking Dutch to transfer a few planes
	id = holhis_navair.4
	title = holhis_navair.4.t
	desc = holhis_navair.4.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Planes + doctrines
		name = holhis_navair.4.a
		if = { #Has BBA, No Fighter 1, Fighter < 50
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				NOT = {
					has_tech = basic_small_airframe
				}
				has_equipment = {
					small_plane_airframe < 50
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_0
					amount = 50
					producer = HOL
					variant_name = "Fokker D.XVII"
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = small_plane_airframe_0
				amount = 50
				target = INS
			}
		}
		else_if = { #Has BBA, No Fighter 1, Fighter > 50
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				NOT = {
					has_tech = basic_small_airframe
				}
				has_equipment = {
					small_plane_airframe > 50
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = small_plane_airframe_0
				amount = 50
				target = INS
			}
		}
		else_if = { #Has BBA, Has Fighter 1, Fighter < 50
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				has_equipment = {
					small_plane_airframe < 50
				}
				has_tech = basic_small_airframe
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_1
					amount = 50
					producer = HOL
					variant_name = "Fokker D.XXI"
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = small_plane_airframe_1
				amount = 50
				target = INS
			}
		}
		else_if = { #Has BBA, Has Fighter 1, Fighter > 50
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				has_equipment = {
					small_plane_airframe > 50
				}
				has_tech = basic_small_airframe
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = small_plane_airframe_1
				amount = 50
				target = INS
			}
		}
		else_if = { #No BBA, No Fighter 1, Fighter < 50
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
					HOL = {
						has_tech = basic_small_airframe
					}
				}
				HOL = {
					has_equipment = {
						small_plane_airframe < 50
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_1
					amount = 50
					producer = HOL
					variant_name = "Fokker D.XXI"
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = small_plane_airframe_0
				amount = 50
				target = INS
			}
		}
		else_if = { #No BBA, No Fighter 1, Fighter > 50
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
					HOL = {
						has_tech = basic_small_airframe
					}
				}
				HOL = {
					has_equipment = {
						small_plane_airframe > 50
					}
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = small_plane_airframe_0

				target = INS
			}
		}
		else_if = { #No BBA, Has Fighter 1, Fighter < 50
			limit = {

				HOL = {
					has_tech = basic_small_airframe

			}

				cost_reduction = 0.5
				uses = 2
				category = air_doctrine
			}
		}

			base = 40
		}
	}

			set_country_flag = INS_plane_blueprint
			country_event = { id = holhis_navair.5 hours = 12 }

			target = FROM
			modifier = large_increase
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = large_increase
		}
	}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = medium_increase
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = medium_increase
		}
	}

	option = { #military access granted

		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = INS_timor_granted
		}
		add_political_power = -50

		}

country_event = { #290 - Hidden effect to setup the historical Japanese occupation
	id = holhis_indonesia.290
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = INS
		has_war_with = JAP
		335 = { is_controlled_by = JAP }
		is_in_faction_with = HOL
		HOL = { has_war_with = JAP }
		surrender_progress > 0.7
		JAP = { #only fascism or neutrality
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Hirohito"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		has_civil_war = no
		#Don't fire if Japan is almost capitulated
		NOT = {
			any_state = {
				is_on_continent = asia
				NOT = { state = 282 }
				NOT = { state = 528 }
				NOT = { state = 529 }
				NOT = { state = 531 }
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_owned_by = JAP
			}
		}		

		#Don't fire if Surabaya, Medan, Manado, and Balikpapan are still secured
		NOT = {
			any_country = {
				is_ai = no
				NOT = { tag = JAP }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
				has_war_with = ROOT
				any_state = {
					is_on_continent = asia
					NOT = { state = 334 } #Balikpapan
					NOT = { state = 672 } #Medan
					NOT = { state = 1021 } #Soerabaja
					NOT = { state = 1025 } #Manado
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_controlled_by = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	immediate = {
		country_event = {
			id = holhis_indonesia.29
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #29 - Fall of the East Indies
	id = holhis_indonesia.29
	title = holhis_indonesia.29.t
	desc = holhis_indonesia.29.d

		}

					limit = {

							is_controlled_by = INJ
						}
					}

				}
				set_rule = { 
					can_join_factions = no

					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no

			}

					set_nationality = INJ

	desc = holhis_japindo.6.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = JAP
		}
		OR = {
			is_puppet_of = HOL
			is_in_faction_with = HOL
		}
		HOL = {
			OR = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = neutrality
			}
		}
		USA = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_defensive_war_with = JAP
		}
	}

	option = { # No

			value = -0.5
		}

	}

				days = 365
			}
		}

			}

			}
		}
		if = {

			}
			remove_ideas = INS_japanese_investment_3
			add_timed_idea = {

			}
		}
		INS = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = USA enemy = JAP hostility_reason = asked_to_join } }
	}
}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_capital = { state = 1020 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = INS_secret_weapon_production
				}
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = -2 }
				672 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				1018 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = INS_civil_war_ongoing
			set_global_flag = INS_civil_war_end
		}
	}

	# Disband the Militias
	option = {
		name = holhis_nationalists.6.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.05 }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Indonesian Militias" }
	}

	# Integrate the Militias
	option = {
		name = holhis_nationalists.6.b
		add_political_power = 75
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		set_division_template_lock = { division_template = "Indonesian Militias" is_locked = no }
	}
}

country_event = { #Nationalists 8 - Dispatcher for uprisings
	id = holhis_nationalists.8
	title = holhis_nationalists.8.t
	desc = holhis_nationalists.8.d

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #They have risen up
		name = holhis_nationalists.8.a
		IF = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = INS_civil_war_ongoing } # No point in kicking off if war has ended already
			random_list = {
				75 = { } # Nothing happens 
				# the "Western" Front
				15 = { # Atjeh uprising
					modifier = {
						add = INS_civil_war_weeks
						always = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5 # To keep Atjeh uprising always slightly more likely than the others
						always = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = { 
							has_country_flag = atj_uprising_flag
							ATJ = { exists = yes }
						}
					}
					set_variable = { INS_nationalist_country = ATJ }
					set_country_flag = atj_uprising_flag
					INS = { country_event = holhis_nationalists.9 }
				}
				# the "Eastern" Front
				10 = { # Molukker uprising
					modifier = {
						add = INS_civil_war_weeks
						always = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = { 
							has_country_flag = mlk_uprising_flag
							MLK = { exists = yes }
						}
					}
					set_variable = { INS_nationalist_country = MLK }
					set_country_flag = mlk_uprising_flag
					INS = { country_event = holhis_nationalists.9 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
				set_country_flag = INS_pardi_admiral_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = INS_wardiman_officer_flag
					}
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_wardiman
					advisor = {
						slot = air_chief
						idea_token = INS_wardiman
						ledger = air
						traits = {
							air_chief_reform_1
						}
						cost = 100
					}
				}
				INS_wardiman = {
					set_portraits = {
						army = {
							small = GFX_idea_indonesia_wardiman
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = INS_wardiman_officer_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = INS_soerjadarma_officer_flag
					}
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_soerjadarma
					advisor = {
						slot = air_chief
						idea_token = INS_soerjadarma
						ledger = air
						traits = {
							air_chief_night_operations_1
						}
						cost = 100
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = INS_soerjadarma_officer_flag
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Commies 13 - End of the Revolution
	id = holhis_commies.13
	title = holhis_commies.13.t
	desc = holhis_commies.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fascists_posing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_capital = { state = 1021 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = INS_secret_weapon_production
				}
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = -2 }
			}
			clr_global_flag = INS_civil_war_ongoing
			set_global_flag = INS_civil_war_end
		}
	}

	# Disband the Militias
	option = {
		name = holhis_commies.13.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = -0.05 }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Indonesian Militias" }
	}

	# Integrate the Militias
	option = {
		name = holhis_commies.13.b
		add_political_power = 75
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		set_division_template_lock = { division_template = "Indonesian Militias" is_locked = no }
	}
}

				}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 35
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 5
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 35
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 65
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_war = yes
				FROM = {
					has_war = no
				}
			}
			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				FROM = {
					is_major = yes
				}
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						is_subject = yes
						is_in_faction = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = holhis_commies.17 hours = 6 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Commies 16 - Faction leader demanded us to reorient our party
	id = holhis_commies.16
	title = holhis_commies.16.t
	desc = holhis_commies.16.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Muso Munawar leads, purge the current leader
		name = holhis_commies.16.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				PREV = {
					has_country_leader_ideology = stalinism
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader_ideology = stalinism
				}
			}
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = INS_RED3
		promote_character = INS_moesso_moenawar
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		PREV = {
			add_to_faction = INS
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "INS"
				value = 200
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Tan Malaka leads, purge the current leader
		name = holhis_commies.16.b
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				PREV = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = marxism
						has_country_leader_ideology = leninism
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = marxism
						has_country_leader_ideology = leninism
					}
				}
			}
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = INS_RED2
		promote_character = INS_tan_malaka
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		PREV = {
			add_to_faction = INS
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "INS"
				value = 200
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Denounce their alliance, create our own
		name = holhis_commies.16.c
		set_cosmetic_tag = INS_RED2
		hidden_effect = {
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = INS_a_distant_ally
				uncomplete_children = yes
				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.075
		add_political_power = 75
		complete_national_focus = INS_asian_commune
		PREV = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "INS"
				value = -200
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Commies 35 - 4th PKI National Congress - 1940-1945
	id = holhis_commies.35
	title = holhis_commies.35.t
	desc = holhis_commies.35.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_indonesian_masses

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Muso - First Term
		name = holhis_commies.35.a
		trigger = {
			INS_moesso_moenawar = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Moesso Moenawar"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = INS_RED3
		promote_character = INS_moesso_moenawar
		add_war_support = 0.075
		add_field_marshal_role = {
			character = INS_moesso_moenawar
			traits = { politically_connected }
			skill = 1
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 1
			planning_skill = 1
			logistics_skill = 1
			legacy_id = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			INS_moesso_moenawar = {
				set_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag
			}
			country_event = { id = holhis_commies.36 days = 1825 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Muso - Second Term
		name = holhis_commies.35.b
		trigger = {
			INS_moesso_moenawar = {
				has_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Moesso Moenawar"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			INS_moesso_moenawar = {
				set_character_flag = INS_second_term_flag
			}
			country_event = { id = holhis_commies.36 days = 1825 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Tan Malaka - First Term
		name = holhis_commies.35.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOS
			}
			INS_tan_malaka = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Tan Malaka"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = INS_RED2
		promote_character = INS_tan_malaka
		add_field_marshal_role = {
			character = INS_tan_malaka
			traits = { guerilla_fighter }
			skill = 2
			attack_skill = 1
			defense_skill = 1
			planning_skill = 2
			logistics_skill = 2
			legacy_id = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			INS_tan_malaka = {
				set_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag
			}
			country_event = { id = holhis_commies.36 days = 1825 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Tan Malaka - Second term
		name = holhis_commies.35.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOS
			}
			INS_tan_malaka = {
				has_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {

					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05

			}
			country_event = { id = holhis_commies.36 days = 1825 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Amir - First term
		name = holhis_commies.35.e
		trigger = {
			INS_amir_sjarifoeddin = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag }
			}
		}

		if = {

					ruling_only = yes
				}

country_event = { #Commies 36 - 5th PKI National Congress - 1945-1950

	title = holhis_commies.36.t
	desc = holhis_commies.36.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_indonesian_masses

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #Muso - First Term
		name = holhis_commies.36.a
		trigger = {
			INS_moesso_moenawar = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag
						has_character_flag = INS_second_term_flag
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Moesso Moenawar"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = INS_RED3
		promote_character = INS_moesso_moenawar
		add_war_support = 0.075
		add_field_marshal_role = {
			character = INS_moesso_moenawar
			traits = { politically_connected }
			skill = 1
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 1
			planning_skill = 1
			logistics_skill = 1
			legacy_id = -1

			character = INS_tan_malaka
			traits = { guerilla_fighter }
			skill = 2
			attack_skill = 1
			defense_skill = 1
			planning_skill = 2
			logistics_skill = 2
			legacy_id = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			INS_tan_malaka = {
				set_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Tan Malaka - Second term
		name = holhis_commies.38.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = SOS
			}
			INS_tan_malaka = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = INS_second_term_flag }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Tan Malaka"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				add_war_support = 0.05
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = INS_RED2
			INS_tan_malaka = {
				set_character_flag = INS_second_term_flag
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
			}
			remove_ideas = INS_gerindo_militias_positive
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Amir - First term
		name = holhis_commies.38.e
		trigger = {
			INS_amir_sjarifoeddin = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = INS_first_term_flag
						has_character_flag = INS_second_term_flag
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {

	title = holhis_commies.101.t
	desc = holhis_commies.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Give them a lot
		name = holhis_commies.101.a
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 40
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = {
				infantry_equipment > 199
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = INS_civil_war_start }
			}
			add_to_array = {
				array = INS.many_weapons_array
				value = ROOT
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = -200
			}
		}
		ELSE = {
			# If war is raging, just send the stuff
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = infantry_equipment
				amount = 200
				target = INS
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_commies.102

				random_days = 5
			}
		}

country_event = { #Gerindo 1 - Formation of Gerindo
	id = holhis_gerindo.1
	title = holhis_gerindo.1.t
	desc = holhis_gerindo.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_amir_sjarifoeddin

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		date > 1937.05.23
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = INS_discourage_democratic_reforms
		}
	}

	option = { #Arrest!
		name = holhis_gerindo.1.a
		add_political_power = -5
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism 
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Allow them
		name = holhis_gerindo.1.b
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = communism
			long_name = INS_communism_party_volksraad_long
			name = INS_communism_party_volksraad
		}
		INS_amir_sjarifoeddin = {
			promote_character = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = INS_gerindo_allowed_flag
		add_political_power = 5
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism 
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
	}
}

				limit = {
					is_owned_by = INS

					}

						OR = {
							is_core_of = ATJ
							is_core_of = PPA
							is_core_of = MLK
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = DFS

			}
		}
	}

		name = holhis_nsb.7.a

		add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "National Socialist Brigade" }

		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		set_division_template_lock = { division_template = "National Socialist Brigade" is_locked = no }
	}
}

				}
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = INS.motorized_equipment_array
				value = weapons_country
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = motorized_equipment
					amount = 100
					producer = var:weapons_country
				}
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = INS.support_equipment_array
				value = weapons_country
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 75
					producer = var:weapons_country
				}
			}
			for_each_loop = {
				array = INS.artillery_equipment_array
				value = weapons_country
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 100
					producer = var:weapons_country
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = INS_get_trucks_flag
				}
				set_technology = { motorised_infantry = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = INS_get_artys_flag
				}
				set_technology = { gw_artillery = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = INS_get_meds_flag
				}
				set_technology = { tech_support = 1 }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = INS_neutrality_party_islam_long
				name = INS_neutrality_party_islam
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = INS_abikoesno_tjokrosoejoso
				country_leader = {
					desc = INS_abikoesno_tjokrosoejoso_desc
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = rexism
					traits = {
						shadow_of_tjokroaminoto_f
					}
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = INS_pni_long
				name = INS_pni
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = INS_soekarno
				country_leader = {
					desc = INS_soekarno_desc
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = centrism
					traits = {
						overzealous_idealist
					}
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			add_advisor_role = {
				character = INS_ernest_douwes_dekker
				advisor = {
					slot = high_command
					idea_token = INS_ernest_douwes_dekker_command
					traits = {
						army_regrouping_1
					}
					cost = 75
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = INS_oerip_general
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = INS_oerip_general
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					character = INS_oerip_soemohardjo
					traits = { unyielding_defender jungle_rat guerilla_fighter inflexible_strategist }
					skill = 2
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 1
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_oerip_soemohardjo
					advisor = {
						slot = high_command
						idea_token = INS_oerip_soemohardjo
						traits = {
							army_logistics_2
						}
						cost = 50
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = INS_gatot_general
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = INS_gatot_general
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					character = INS_gatot_soebroto
					traits = { defensive_doctrine jungle_rat }
					skill = 1
					attack_skill = 1
					defense_skill = 2
					planning_skill = 1
					logistics_skill = 2
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_gatot_soebroto
					advisor = {
						slot = army_chief
						idea_token = INS_gatot_soebroto
						ledger = army
						traits = {
							army_chief_defensive_1
						}
						cost = 50
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = INS_pardi_admiral_flag
					}
				}
				add_naval_commander_role = {
					character = INS_mas_pardi
					traits = { bold }
					skill = 1
					attack_skill = 2
					defense_skill = 1
					maneuvering_skill = 1
					coordination_skill = 1
					legacy_id = -1
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_mas_pardi
					advisor = {
						slot = navy_chief
						idea_token = INS_mas_pardi
						ledger = navy
						traits = {
							navy_chief_maneuver_1
						}
						cost = 75
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = INS_pardi_admiral_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = INS_wardiman_officer_flag
					}
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_wardiman
					advisor = {
						slot = air_chief
						idea_token = INS_wardiman
						ledger = air
						traits = {
							air_chief_reform_1
						}
						cost = 100
					}
				}
				INS_wardiman = {
					set_portraits = {
						army = {
							small = GFX_idea_indonesia_wardiman
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = INS_wardiman_officer_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = INS_soerjadarma_officer_flag
					}
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_soerjadarma

						ledger = air

							air_chief_night_operations_1
						}
						cost = 100
					}

		}
	}

					has_completed_focus = INS_secret_weapon_production
				}

				672 = {

						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				1018 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = INS_civil_war_ongoing
			set_global_flag = INS_civil_war_end
		}
	}

	# Disband the Militias
	option = {
		name = holhis_volksraad.12.a
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.05 }

	}

	# Integrate the Militias

		name = holhis_volksraad.12.b
		add_political_power = 75
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		set_division_template_lock = { division_template = "Indonesian Militias" is_locked = no }
	}
}

			popularity = -0.015
		}
		add_autonomy_ratio = {
			value = 0.05

		}
	}

	option = { #Put him on house arrest

		add_war_support = 0.01
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic 
			popularity = -0.01
		}

			value = 0.03
		}

		}
	}

country_event = { #Volksraad 180 - Event dispatcher for Thamrin's fate
	id = holhis_volksraad.180

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = INS_thamrin_locked_up
			has_country_flag = INS_thamrin_house_arrest
		}
	}

	immediate = { #Make it 80-20 if Thamrin is locked up, but 50-50 if Thamrin is only on house arrest
		random_list = {
			80 = { #Thamrin died in prison - Historical
				INS = {
					country_event = { id = holhis_volksraad.19 days = 4 random_days = 3 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_country_flag = INS_thamrin_house_arrest
				}
			}
			20 = { #Thamrin died in his house
				INS = {
					country_event = { id = holhis_volksraad.20 days = 6 random_days = 4 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_country_flag = INS_thamrin_locked_up
				}
			}
			20 = { #Thamrin survives
				INS = {
					country_event = { id = holhis_volksraad.21 days = 6 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Round Table 2 - Conference - Dutch Side
	id = holhis_roundtable.2
	title = holhis_roundtable.2.t
	desc = holhis_roundtable.2.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Hand over everything
		name = holhis_roundtable.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = INS_NATREV_full_handover_tt
		INS = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = HOL
							is_subject_of = HOL
							is_in_faction_with = HOL
						}
					}
				}
				CONTROLLER = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		INS = {
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_roundtable.3
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_truce = {
				target = INS
				days = 730
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #We hold West Papua
		name = holhis_roundtable.2.b
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 669
			controls_state = 1028
			controls_state = 1029
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = INS_NATREV_two_third_handover_tt
		INS = {
			country_event = { id = holhis_roundtable.4 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Council 1 - Ranneft retires
	id = holhis_council.1

	desc = holhis_council.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_raad_van_indie

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		has_government = neutrality
		date > 1936.06.28
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		focus_progress = {
			focus = INS_continue_reform
			progress > 0
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	option = { #Bussche

		retire_character = INS_meyer_ranneft

		add_ideas = INS_cornelis_bussche
		custom_effect_tooltip = holhis_vp_cons_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = holhis_council.2 days = 14 random_days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = holhis_council.6 days = 730 random_days = 182 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	option = { #Wait
		name = holhis_council.1.b
		add_stability = -0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_waiting_for_tjarda
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Council 4 - Second voting for Raad van Indie
	id = holhis_council.4
	title = holhis_council.4.t
	desc = holhis_council.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ins_raad_van_indie

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		has_government = neutrality
		date > 1936.08.06
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = INS_discourage_democratic_reforms }
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Tjarda van Starkenborgh"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = INS_waiting_for_tjarda
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 21 }

	option = { #Bussche
		name = holhis_council.4.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_meyer_ranneft
			}
			retire_character = INS_meyer_ranneft
		}
		add_ideas = INS_cornelis_bussche
		custom_effect_tooltip = holhis_vp_cons_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_raad_vp_bussche
			set_country_flag = INS_ranneft_retired
			country_event = { id = holhis_council.2 days = 14 random_days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = holhis_council.6 days = 730 random_days = 182 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Ranneft as Advisor
		name = holhis_council.4.b
		add_political_power = -50
		add_ideas = INS_cornelis_bussche
		custom_effect_tooltip = holhis_vp_mods_tt
		INS_meyer_ranneft = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_country_leader_traits = {
					remove = raad_indie_ranneft
					add = colonial_reformer
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = liberal_journalist
				}
				remove_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = independent_journalist
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
				character = INS_meyer_ranneft 
				value = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = INS_raad_vp_bussche
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = holhis_council.2 days = 14 random_days = 7 }
			country_event = { id = holhis_council.6 days = 730 random_days = 60 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Visman
		name = holhis_council.4.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = INS_raad_member_visman
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_meyer_ranneft
			}
			retire_character = INS_meyer_ranneft
		}
		INS_frans_visman = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_country_leader_traits = {
					remove = colonial_reformer2
					add = raad_indie_visman
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = raad_indie_visman
				}
				remove_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = colonial_reformer2
				}
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					character = INS_frans_visman 
					value = no
				}
			}
		}
		add_ideas = INS_frans_visman
		custom_effect_tooltip = holhis_vp_mods_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_raad_vp_visman
		}
	}
}

			remove_ideas = INS_cornelis_bussche

	}

	option = { #Let him stay
		name = holhis_council.9.b
		INS = {
			HOL_jacques_de_kadt = {
				set_character_flag = INS_de_kadt_accepted
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = HOL_jacques_de_kadt
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_political_power = -10
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

			}

		}
	}

country_event = { #Aging 1 - Syahrir
	id = holhis_aging.1
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		OR = {
			date > 1944.03.05
			AND = {
				date > 1939.03.05
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = INS_expel_the_colonials
					has_completed_focus = INS_merdeka
				}
			}
		}
		INS_soetan_sjahrir = {
			has_trait = silent_mule
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = INS_soetan_sjahrir
			}
			set_country_flag = INS_sjahrir_stays
		}
		INS_soetan_sjahrir = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_country_leader_traits = {
					remove = silent_mule
					add = silent_workhorse
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = silent_workhorse
				}
				remove_trait = {
					slot = political_advisor
					trait = silent_mule
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = INS_sjahrir_stays
			}
			activate_advisor = INS_soetan_sjahrir
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Aging 8 - Jan Hendrik Wesseling
	id = holhis_aging.8
	title = holhis_aging.8.t
	desc = holhis_aging.8.desc

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		date > 1939.01.01
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		has_character = INS_wesseling
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = { #if not at war, he can be retired from field duty
		name = holhis_aging.8.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = INS_wesseling_retiring_age_flag
			}
		}
		INS_wesseling = {
			remove_unit_leader_role = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_wesseling_retiring_age_flag
			set_country_flag = INS_wesseling_retired_flag
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_aging.8
				days = 1826
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #if at war, we can extend his service with a bit of cost; if not, extending it would cost a few more
		name = holhis_aging.8.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = INS_wesseling_extended_flag
					has_country_flag = INS_wesseling_retiring_age_flag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = no
				}
				has_political_power > 14
				command_power > 19
				has_army_experience > 19
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = no
			}
			add_political_power = -15
			add_command_power = -20
			army_experience = -20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			add_political_power = -5
			add_command_power = -10
			army_experience = -5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_wesseling_retiring_age_flag
			set_country_flag = INS_wesseling_extended_flag
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_aging.8
				days = 1826
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #War or not, if he's 60, he's retired. But he can be also retired early
		name = holhis_aging.8.c
		retire_character = INS_wesseling
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = INS_wesseling_retiring_age_flag
				}
			}
			add_command_power = 5
			army_experience = 10
		}
	}
}

	option = { #War or not, if he's 60, he's retired. But he can be also retired early
		name = holhis_aging.10.c
		retire_character = INS_elshout
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = INS_elshout_retiring_age_flag
				}
			}
			add_command_power = 5
			army_experience = 10
		}
		set_country_flag = INS_elshout_retired_flag
	}
}

country_event = { #Aging 11 - Tjalling Bakker
	id = holhis_aging.11
	title = holhis_aging.11.t
	desc = holhis_aging.11.desc

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		date > 1941.01.01
		has_character = INS_tjalling
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = { #if not at war, he can be retired from field duty
		name = holhis_aging.11.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = INS_tjalling_retiring_age_flag
			}
		}
		INS_tjalling = {
			remove_unit_leader_role = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_tjalling_retiring_age_flag
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_aging.11
				days = 1826
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #if at war, we can extend his service with a bit of cost; if not, extending it would cost a few more
		name = holhis_aging.11.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = INS_tjalling_extended_flag
					has_country_flag = INS_tjalling_retiring_age_flag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = no
				}
				has_political_power > 14
				command_power > 19
				has_army_experience > 19
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = no
			}
			add_political_power = -15
			add_command_power = -20
			army_experience = -20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			add_political_power = -5
			add_command_power = -10
			army_experience = -5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_tjalling_retiring_age_flag
			set_country_flag = INS_tjalling_extended_flag
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_aging.11
				days = 1826
			}
		}
	}

			limit = {

			army_experience = 10
		}

			army_experience = -5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_hendrik_uhl_retiring_age_flag
			set_country_flag = INS_hendrik_uhl_extended_flag
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_aging.19
				days = 1826
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #War or not, if he's 60, he's retired. But he can be also retired early
		name = holhis_aging.19.c
		retire_character = INS_hendrik_uhl
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = INS_hendrik_uhl_retiring_age_flag
				}
			}
			add_command_power = 5
			army_experience = 10
		}
	}
}

	id = holhis_aging.20
	title = holhis_aging.20.t
	desc = holhis_aging.20.d

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		date > 1947.7.14
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = INS_local_militias
			has_completed_focus = INS_strict_hierarchy
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = INS_flexible_navy
			has_completed_focus = INS_dominant_navy
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holhis_aging.20.a
		add_naval_commander_role = {
			character = INS_soebijakto
			traits = { fleet_protector }
			skill = 1
			attack_skill = 1
			defense_skill = 2
			maneuvering_skill = 1
			coordination_skill = 1
			legacy_id = -1
		}
		add_advisor_role = {
			character = INS_soebijakto
			advisor = {
				slot = navy_chief
				idea_token = INS_soebijakto
				ledger = navy
				traits = {
					navy_chief_decisive_battle_1
				}
				cost = 75
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Aging 23 - Van Dulm
	id = holhis_aging.23
	title = holhis_aging.23.t
	desc = holhis_aging.23.desc

	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = INS
		date > 1936.03.01
		has_start_date < 1936.01.02
		has_character = INS_maarten_van_dulm
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = { #if not at war, he can be retired from field duty
		name = holhis_aging.19.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = INS_maarten_van_dulm_retiring_age_flag
			}
		}
		INS_maarten_van_dulm = {
			remove_unit_leader_role = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_maarten_van_dulm_retiring_age_flag
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_aging.23
				days = 1251
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #if at war, we can extend his service with a bit of cost; if not, extending it would cost a few more
		name = holhis_aging.23.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = INS_maarten_van_dulm_extended_flag
					has_country_flag = INS_maarten_van_dulm_retiring_age_flag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = no
				}
				has_political_power > 14
				command_power > 19
				has_navy_experience > 19
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war = yes
				}
				has_political_power > 4
				command_power > 9
				has_navy_experience > 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = no
			}
			add_political_power = -15
			add_command_power = -20
			navy_experience = -20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			add_political_power = -5
			add_command_power = -10
			navy_experience = -5
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = INS_maarten_van_dulm_retiring_age_flag
			set_country_flag = INS_maarten_van_dulm_extended_flag
			country_event = {
				id = holhis_aging.23
				days = 1251
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #War or not, if he's 60, he's retired. But he can be also retired early
		name = holhis_aging.23.c
		retire_character = INS_maarten_van_dulm
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = INS_maarten_van_dulm_retiring_age_flag
				}
			}
			add_command_power = 5
			navy_experience = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Arabia formable - choose capital
	id = holhis_history.7
	title = holhis_history.7.t
	desc = holhis_history.7.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_ast_parliament_house

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = holhis_history.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		set_capital = { state = 291 } #Baghdad
		set_victory_points = {
			province = 2097
			value = 15
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
			set_compliance = 50
		}
		set_global_flag = arabia_move_capital
	}

	option = {
		name = holhis_history.7.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		set_capital = { state = 856 } #Makkah
		set_victory_points = {
			province = 5037
			value = 15
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
			set_compliance = 50
		}
		set_global_flag = arabia_move_capital
	}

	option = {
		name = holhis_history.7.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		set_capital = { state = 554 } #Damascus
		set_victory_points = {
			province = 4111
			value = 15
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
			set_compliance = 50
		}
		set_global_flag = arabia_move_capital
	}

	option = {
		name = holhis_history.7.d
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # ROM becomes just Wallachia
	id = holhis_history.8
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		owns_state = 46 #still holding Muntenia
		country_exists = TRA
		country_exists = MOL
		MOL = {
			owns_state = 79
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = ROM_became_wallachia }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		set_cosmetic_tag = ROM_wallachia
		set_global_flag = ROM_became_wallachia
	}
}

country_event = { # ROM becomes ROM again
	id = holhis_history.9
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		owns_state = 79 #hold Muntenia
		owns_state = 46 #hold Moldavia
		has_global_flag = ROM_became_wallachia
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }

	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		clr_global_flag = ROM_became_wallachia
	}
}
